height="277"
class="thumbimage"
srcset="http://rpmedia.ask.com/ts?u=/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/78/Deep_Purple_%281985%29.jpg/300px-Deep_Purple_%281985%29.jpg
1.5x,
http://rpmedia.ask.com/ts?u=/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/78/Deep_Purple_%281985%29.jpg/400px-Deep_Purple_%281985%29.jpg
2x"
/></a>










<div
class="thumbcaption">











<div
class="magnify">











<a
href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/File:Deep_Purple_(1985).jpg"
target="_blank"
class="internal"
title="Enlarge"><img
src="http://sp.ask.com/sh/i/wiki/magnify-clip.png"
width="15"
height="11"
alt=""
/></a>










</div>
Deep
Purple
at
the











<a
href="/wiki/Cow_Palace?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Cow
Palace">Cow
Palace</a>,
San
Francisco,
California.
January
1985









</div>









</div>








</div>








<p>The
Mark
II
line-up
then
released
<i><a
href="/wiki/The_House_of_Blue_Light?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
House
of
Blue
Light">The
House
of
Blue
Light</a></i>
in
1987,
which
was
followed
by
a
world
tour
(interrupted
after
Blackmore
broke
a
finger
on
stage
while
trying
to
catch
his
guitar
after
throwing
it
in
the
air)
and
another
live
album
<i><a
href="/wiki/Nobody%27s_Perfect_(Deep_Purple_album)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Nobody's
Perfect
(Deep
Purple
album)">Nobody's
Perfect</a></i>
(1988)
which
was
culled
from
several
shows
on
this
tour,
but
still
largely
based
on
the
by-now
familiar
<i>Made
in
Japan</i>
set-list.
In
the
UK
a
new
version
of
&quot;Hush&quot;
(with
Gillan
on
lead
vocals)
was
released
to
mark
20
years
of
the
band.
In
1989
Gillan
was
fired
as
his
relations
with
Blackmore
had
again
soured
and
their
musical
differences
had
diverged
too
far.
Originally,
the
band
intended
to
recruit
<a
href="/wiki/Survivor_(band)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Survivor
(band)">Survivor</a>
frontman
<a
href="/wiki/Jimi_Jamison?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Jimi
Jamison">Jimi
Jamison</a>
as
Gillan's
replacement,
but
this
fell
through
due
to
complications
with
<a
href="/wiki/Scotti_Brothers_Records?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Scotti
Brothers
Records">Jamison's
record
label</a>.<sup
id="cite_ref-aor.nu_83-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-aor.nu-83"><span>[</span>83<span>]</span></a></sup><sup
id="cite_ref-picturedwithtin.com_84-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-picturedwithtin.com-84"><span>[</span>84<span>]</span></a></sup>
Eventually,
after
auditioning
several
high-profile
candidates,
including
<a
href="/wiki/Brian_Howe_(singer)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Brian
Howe
(singer)">Brian
Howe</a>
(<a
href="/wiki/White_Spirit_(band)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="White
Spirit
(band)">White
Spirit</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Ted_Nugent?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Ted
Nugent">Ted
Nugent</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Bad_Company?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Bad
Company">Bad
Company</a>),
<a
href="/wiki/Doug_Pinnick?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Doug
Pinnick">Doug
Pinnick</a>
(<a
href="/wiki/King%27s_X?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="King's
X">King's
X</a>),
Australians
<a
href="/wiki/Jimmy_Barnes?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Jimmy
Barnes">Jimmy
Barnes</a>
(<a
href="/wiki/Cold_Chisel?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Cold
Chisel">Cold
Chisel</a>)
and
<a
href="/wiki/John_Farnham?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="John
Farnham">John
Farnham</a>
(<a
href="/wiki/Little_River_Band?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Little
River
Band">Little
River
Band</a>),
Terry
Brock
(Strangeways,
<a
href="/wiki/Giant_(band)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Giant
(band)">Giant</a>)
and
Norman
&quot;Kal&quot;
Swann
(<a
href="/wiki/Tytan_(band)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Tytan
(band)">Tytan</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Lion_(band)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Lion
(band)">Lion</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Bad_Moon_Rising_(band)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Bad
Moon
Rising
(band)">Bad
Moon
Rising</a>),<sup
id="cite_ref-Thompson2004pp259_85-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Thompson2004pp259-85"><span>[</span>85<span>]</span></a></sup>
former
Rainbow
vocalist
<a
href="/wiki/Joe_Lynn_Turner?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Joe
Lynn
Turner">Joe
Lynn
Turner</a>
was
recruited
into
the
band.
This
Mark
V
line-up
recorded
just
one
album,
<i><a
href="/wiki/Slaves_%26_Masters?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Slaves
&amp;
Masters"
class="mw-redirect">Slaves
&amp;
Masters</a></i>
(1990)
and
toured
in
support.
It
achieved
modest
success
and
reached
number
87
on
the
Billboard
Charts
in
the
US,<sup
id="cite_ref-AllMusic.com_78-1"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-AllMusic.com-78"><span>[</span>78<span>]</span></a></sup>
but
some
fans
criticised
it
as
little
more
than
a
so-called
&quot;generic
<a
href="/wiki/Foreigner_(band)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Foreigner
(band)">Foreigner</a>
wannabe&quot;
album.<sup
id="cite_ref-86"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-86"><span>[</span>86<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>With
the
tour
complete,
Turner
was
forced
out,
as
Lord,
Paice
and
Glover
(and
the
record
company)
wanted
Gillan
back
in
the
fold
for
the
25th
anniversary.
Blackmore
grudgingly
relented,
after
requesting
and
eventually
receiving
250,000
dollars
in
his
bank
account<sup
id="cite_ref-87"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-87"><span>[</span>87<span>]</span></a></sup>
and
the
classic
line-up
recorded
<i><a
href="/wiki/The_Battle_Rages_On...?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Battle
Rages
On...">The
Battle
Rages
On...</a></i>.
However,
Gillan
reworked
much
of
the
existing
material
which
had
been
written
with
Turner
for
the
album.
As
a
result,
Blackmore
became
infuriated
at
what
he
considered
non-melodic
elements.<sup
id="cite_ref-88"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-88"><span>[</span>88<span>]</span></a></sup>
During
an
otherwise
successful
European
tour,
Blackmore
walked
out
in
1993,
for
good,
during
a
17
November
show
in
Helsinki,
Finland.<sup
id="cite_ref-BBC_Deep_Purple_89-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-BBC_Deep_Purple-89"><span>[</span>89<span>]</span></a></sup>
<a
href="/wiki/Joe_Satriani?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Joe
Satriani">Joe
Satriani</a>
was
drafted
to
complete
the
Japanese
dates
in
December
and
stayed
on
for
a
European
Summer
tour
in
1994.
He
was
asked
to
join
permanently,
but
his
commitments
to
his
contract
with
<a
href="/wiki/Epic_Records?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Epic
Records">Epic
Records</a>
prevented
this.
The
band
unanimously
chose
<a
href="/wiki/Dixie_Dregs?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Dixie
Dregs">Dixie
Dregs</a>/<a
href="/wiki/Kansas_(band)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Kansas
(band)">Kansas</a>
guitarist
<a
href="/wiki/Steve_Morse?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Steve
Morse">Steve
Morse</a>
to
become
Satriani's
successor.<sup
id="cite_ref-90"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-90"><span>[</span>90<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<h3><span
class="mw-headline"
id="Revival_with_Steve_Morse_and_longer_tours_.281994.E2.80.93present.29">Revival
with
Steve
Morse
and
longer
tours
(1994–present)</span>
<span
class="mw-editsection">[<a
href="/wiki?title=Deep_Purple&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8"
title="Edit
section:
Revival
with
Steve
Morse
and
longer
tours
(1994–present)">edit</a>]</span></h3>








<div
class="quotebox"
style="float:
right;
clear:
right;
margin:
0.5em
0
0.8em
1.4em;
width:
35%;
padding:
6px;
border:
1px
solid
#aaa;
font-size:
88%;
background-color:
#F9F9F9;">









<div
style="position:
relative;
text-align:
left;">










<div>











<p>Deep
Purple
was
approaching
death
in
1993.
Audiences
were
falling
off,
we
were
playing
4,000-seaters
with
barely
1200,
1500
people
in
them.&nbsp;...
Then,
fortunately,
Ritchie
walked
out,
the
sun
shone
again
and
we
all
said:
&quot;OK,
we'll
give
it
one
more
shot.&quot;
So,
yes,
we
are
grateful
for
that
chance.</p>










</div>









</div>









<div
style="text-align:
left;">









--Ian
Gillan,
on
the
band's
rebirth









<sup
id="cite_ref-sun2007_91-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-sun2007-91"><span>[</span>91<span>]</span></a></sup>








</div>








</div>

class="thumb
tright">









<div
class="thumbinner"
style="width:227px;">

/></a>










<div
class="thumbcaption">











<div

<a

</div>











<a
href="/wiki/Roger_Glover?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Roger
Glover">Roger
Glover</a>
and











<a
href="/wiki/Steve_Morse?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Steve
Morse">Steve
Morse</a>
playing
the
intro
to
&quot;










<a
href="/wiki/Highway_Star_(song)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Highway
Star
(song)">Highway
Star</a>&quot;
at
the











<a
href="/wiki/Molson_Amphitheatre?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Molson
Amphitheatre"
class="mw-redirect">Molson
Amphitheatre</a>,
Toronto,
Canada,
2005









</div>









</div>








</div>








<p>Morse's
arrival
revitalised
the
band
creatively,
and
in
1996
a
new
album
titled
<i><a
href="/wiki/Purpendicular?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Purpendicular">Purpendicular</a></i>
was
released,
showing
a
wide
variety
of
musical
styles,
though
it
never
made
chart
success
on
Billboard
200
in
the
US.<sup
id="cite_ref-AllMusic.com_78-2"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-AllMusic.com-78"><span>[</span>78<span>]</span></a></sup>
The
Mark
VII
line-up
then
released
a
new
live
album
<i><a
href="/wiki/Live_at_The_Olympia_%2796?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Live
at
The
Olympia
'96">Live
at
The
Olympia
'96</a></i>
in
1997.
With
a
revamped
set
list
to
tour,
Deep
Purple
enjoyed
successful
tours
throughout
the
rest
of
the
1990s,
releasing
the
harder-sounding
<i><a
href="/wiki/Abandon_(album)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Abandon
(album)">Abandon</a></i>
in
1998,
and
touring
with
renewed
enthusiasm.
In
1999,
Lord,
with
the
help
of
a
Dutch
fan,
who
was
also
a
musicologist
and
composer,
<a
href="/wiki/Marco_de_Goeij?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Marco
de
Goeij">Marco
de
Goeij</a>,
painstakingly
recreated
the
<i><a
href="/wiki/Concerto_for_Group_and_Orchestra?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Concerto
for
Group
and
Orchestra">Concerto
for
Group
and
Orchestra</a></i>,
the
original
score
having
been
lost.
It
was
once
again
performed
at
the
<a
href="/wiki/Royal_Albert_Hall?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Royal
Albert
Hall">Royal
Albert
Hall</a>
in
September
1999,
this
time
with
the
<a
href="/wiki/London_Symphony_Orchestra?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="London
Symphony
Orchestra">London
Symphony
Orchestra</a>
conducted
by
Paul
Mann.<sup
id="cite_ref-Buckley_92-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Buckley-92"><span>[</span>92<span>]</span></a></sup>
The
concert
also
featured
songs
from
each
member's
solo
careers,
as
well
as
a
short
Deep
Purple
set,
and
the
occasion
was
commemorated
on
the
2000
album
<i><a
href="/wiki/Live_at_the_Royal_Albert_Hall_(Deep_Purple_album)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Live
at
the
Royal
Albert
Hall
(Deep
Purple
album)">Live
at
the
Royal
Albert
Hall</a></i>.<sup
id="cite_ref-Buckley_92-1"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Buckley-92"><span>[</span>92<span>]</span></a></sup>
In
2001,
the
<a
href="/wiki/Box_set?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Box
set">box
set</a>
<i><a
href="/wiki/The_Soundboard_Series?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Soundboard
Series">The
Soundboard
Series</a></i>
was
released
featuring
concerts
from
the
2001
Australian
Tour
plus
two
from
Tokyo,
Japan.<sup
id="cite_ref-93"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-93"><span>[</span>93<span>]</span></a></sup></p>

(2006)

<p>Much
of
the
next
few
years
was
spent
on
the
road
touring.
The
group
continued
forward
until
2002,
when
founding
member
Lord
(who,
along
with
Paice,
was
the
only
member
to
be
in
all
incarnations
of
the
band)
announced
his
amicable
retirement
from
the
band
to
pursue
personal
projects
(especially
orchestral
work).
Lord
left
his
<a
href="/wiki/Hammond_organ?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Hammond
organ">Hammond
organ</a>
to
his
replacement,
rock
keyboard
veteran
<a
href="/wiki/Don_Airey?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Don
Airey">Don
Airey</a>
(Rainbow,
Ozzy
Osbourne,
Black
Sabbath,
Whitesnake),
who
had
helped
Deep
Purple
out
when
Lord's
knee
was
injured
in
2001.
In
2003,
Deep
Purple
released
their
first
studio
albums
in
five
years
(<i><a
href="/wiki/Bananas_(album)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Bananas
(album)">Bananas</a></i>)
and
began
touring
in
support
of
the
album.
<a
href="/wiki/EMI_Records?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="EMI
Records">EMI
Records</a>
refused
a
contract
extension
with
Deep
Purple,
possibly
because
of
lower
than
expected
sales.
Actually
<i><a
href="/wiki/In_Concert_with_the_London_Symphony_Orchestra?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="In
Concert
with
the
London
Symphony
Orchestra">In
Concert
with
the
London
Symphony
Orchestra</a></i>
sold
more
than
<i>Bananas</i>.<sup
id="cite_ref-94"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-94"><span>[</span>94<span>]</span></a></sup>
Most
of
the
songs
played
in
their
live
concerts
consist
of
classic
1970s
material.
In
July
2005,
the
band
played
at
the
<a
href="/wiki/Live_8?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Live
8">Live
8</a>
concert
in
<a
href="/wiki/Park_Place_(Ontario)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Park
Place
(Ontario)">Park
Place</a>
(<a
href="/wiki/Barrie,_Ontario?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Barrie,
Ontario"
class="mw-redirect">Barrie,
Ontario</a>)
and,
in
October
released
their
next
album,
<i><a
href="/wiki/Rapture_of_the_Deep?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Rapture
of
the
Deep">Rapture
of
the
Deep</a></i>,
which
was
followed
by
the
<a
href="/wiki/Rapture_of_the_Deep_tour?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Rapture
of
the
Deep
tour">Rapture
of
the
Deep
tour</a>.
This
Mark
VIII
line-up's
two
studio
albums
were
produced
by
<a
href="/wiki/Michael_Bradford?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Michael
Bradford">Michael
Bradford</a>,
who
is
known
as
rap
or
pop
musician.<sup
id="cite_ref-95"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-95"><span>[</span>95<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>In
February
2007,
Gillan
asked
fans
not
to
buy
a
live
album
<i><a
href="/wiki/Come_Hell_or_High_Water?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Come
Hell
or
High
Water">Come
Hell
or
High
Water</a></i>
being
released
by
<a
href="/wiki/Sony_BMG?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Sony
BMG">Sony
BMG</a>.
This
was
a
recording
of
their
1993
appearance
at
the
<a
href="/wiki/National_Exhibition_Centre?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="National
Exhibition
Centre">NEC</a>
in
Birmingham.<sup
id="cite_ref-BBC_Deep_Purple_89-1"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-BBC_Deep_Purple-89"><span>[</span>89<span>]</span></a></sup>
Recordings
of
this
show
have
previously
been
released
without
assistance
from
Gillan
or
any
other
members
of
the
band,
but
he
said:
&quot;It
was
one
of
the
lowest
points
of
my
life
–
all
of
our
lives,
actually&quot;.<sup
id="cite_ref-BBC_Deep_Purple_89-2"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-BBC_Deep_Purple-89"><span>[</span>89<span>]</span></a></sup>
In
2009,
Ian
Gillan
said,
&quot;Record
sales
have
been
steadily
declining,
but
people
are
prepared
to
pay
a
lot
for
concert
tickets.&quot;<sup
id="cite_ref-Gillan_talks_money_96-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Gillan_talks_money-96"><span>[</span>96<span>]</span></a></sup>
In
addition,
Gillan
stated
&quot;I
don't
think
happiness
comes
with
money.&quot;<sup
id="cite_ref-Gillan_talks_money_96-1"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Gillan_talks_money-96"><span>[</span>96<span>]</span></a></sup>
In
2011,
Deep
Purple
did
concert
tours
in
48
countries.<sup
id="cite_ref-New_Studio_Album_Next_Year_97-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-New_Studio_Album_Next_Year-97"><span>[</span>97<span>]</span></a></sup>
<a
href="/wiki/The_Songs_That_Built_Rock_Tour?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Songs
That
Built
Rock
Tour">The
Songs
That
Built
Rock
Tour</a>
featured
a
38-piece
orchestra,
and
included
a
performance
at
London's
<a
href="/wiki/The_O2_Arena_(London)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
O2
Arena
(London)"
class="mw-redirect">O2
Arena</a>.<sup
id="cite_ref-98"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-98"><span>[</span>98<span>]</span></a></sup>
Until
May
2011,
the
band
members
had
disagreed
about
whether
to
make
a
new
studio
album,
because
it
would
not
really
make
money
anymore.
Roger
Glover
stated
that
Deep
Purple
should
make
a
new
studio
album
&quot;even
if
it
costs
us
money.&quot;<sup
id="cite_ref-99"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-99"><span>[</span>99<span>]</span></a></sup></p>

<p>In
early
2011,
David
Coverdale
and
Glenn
Hughes
told
<a
href="/wiki/VH1?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="VH1">VH1</a>
they
would
like
to
reunite
with
former
Deep
Purple
Mark
III
line-up
for
the
right
opportunity,
such
as
a
benefit
concert.<sup
id="cite_ref-100"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-100"><span>[</span>100<span>]</span></a></sup>
The
current
band's
chief
sound
engineer
on
nine
years
of
tours,
Moray
McMillin,
died
in
September
2011,
aged
57.<sup
id="cite_ref-101"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-101"><span>[</span>101<span>]</span></a></sup></p>








<p>After
a
lot
of
songwriting
sessions
in
Europe,<sup
id="cite_ref-TitleAnnounced_102-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-TitleAnnounced-102"><span>[</span>102<span>]</span></a></sup>
Deep
Purple
decided
to
do
recording
through
the
summer
of
2012,
and
the
band
announced
the
release
of
their
new
studio
album
in
2013.<sup
id="cite_ref-New_Studio_Album_Next_Year_97-1"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-New_Studio_Album_Next_Year-97"><span>[</span>97<span>]</span></a></sup>
Steve
Morse
announced
to
French
magazine
<i>Rock
Hard</i>
that
the
new
studio
album
would
be
produced
by
the
highly
respected
<a
href="/wiki/Bob_Ezrin?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Bob
Ezrin">Bob
Ezrin</a>,<sup
id="cite_ref-103"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-103"><span>[</span>103<span>]</span></a></sup>
who
is
known
for
his
works
with
<a
href="/wiki/Alice_Cooper?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Alice
Cooper">Alice
Cooper</a>,
<a
href="/wiki/Kiss_(band)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Kiss
(band)">Kiss</a>,
and
<a
href="/wiki/Pink_Floyd?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Pink
Floyd">Pink
Floyd</a>.
On
16
July
2012,
the
band's
co-founding
member
and
former
organ
player,
Jon
Lord,
died
in
London,
aged
71.<sup
id="cite_ref-104"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-104"><span>[</span>104<span>]</span></a></sup><sup
id="cite_ref-105"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-105"><span>[</span>105<span>]</span></a></sup><sup
id="cite_ref-106"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-106"><span>[</span>106<span>]</span></a></sup>
In

2012,
Roger
Glover
revealed
in
an

that
the
band
has
completed
work
on
14

for
a
new

11

set
to

on

to

id="cite_ref-107"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-107"><span>[</span>107<span>]</span></a></sup><sup
id="cite_ref-108"
class="reference"><a

On

<i><a

<h2><span
class="mw-headline"
id="Legacy">Legacy</span>
<span
class="mw-editsection">[<a
href="/wiki?title=Deep_Purple&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9"
title="Edit
section:
Legacy">edit</a>]</span></h2>








<p>Deep
Purple
are
cited
as
one
of
the
pioneers
of
hard
rock
and
heavy
metal,
along
with
<a
href="/wiki/Led_Zeppelin?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Led
Zeppelin">Led
Zeppelin</a>
and
<a
href="/wiki/Black_Sabbath?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Black
Sabbath">Black
Sabbath</a>.<sup
id="cite_ref-Wasler_2-2"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Wasler-2"><span>[</span>2<span>]</span></a></sup><sup
id="cite_ref-109"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-109"><span>[</span>109<span>]</span></a></sup>
The
group
have
influenced
a
number
of
rock
and
metal
bands
including
<a
href="/wiki/Metallica?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Metallica">Metallica</a>,<sup
id="cite_ref-110"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-110"><span>[</span>110<span>]</span></a></sup>
<a
href="/wiki/Queen_(band)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Queen
(band)">Queen</a>,<sup
id="cite_ref-111"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-111"><span>[</span>111<span>]</span></a></sup>
<a
href="/wiki/Aerosmith?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Aerosmith">Aerosmith</a>,<sup
id="cite_ref-112"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-112"><span>[</span>112<span>]</span></a></sup>
<a
href="/wiki/Van_Halen?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Van
Halen">Van
Halen</a>,<sup
id="cite_ref-113"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-113"><span>[</span>113<span>]</span></a></sup>
<a
href="/wiki/Alice_in_Chains?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Alice
in
Chains">Alice
in
Chains</a>,<sup
id="cite_ref-114"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-114"><span>[</span>114<span>]</span></a></sup>
<a
href="/wiki/Pantera?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Pantera">Pantera</a>,<sup
id="cite_ref-115"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-115"><span>[</span>115<span>]</span></a></sup>
<a
href="/wiki/Bon_Jovi?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Bon
Jovi">Bon
Jovi</a>,<sup
id="cite_ref-116"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-116"><span>[</span>116<span>]</span></a></sup>
<a
href="/wiki/Rush_(band)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Rush
(band)">Rush</a>,<sup
id="cite_ref-117"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-117"><span>[</span>117<span>]</span></a></sup>
<a
href="/wiki/Mot%C3%B6rhead?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Mot&ouml;rhead">Mot&ouml;rhead</a>,<sup
id="cite_ref-118"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-118"><span>[</span>118<span>]</span></a></sup>
and
many
<a

<p>In
2000,
Deep
Purple
were
ranked
number
22
on
<a
href="/wiki/VH1?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="VH1">VH1</a>'s
&quot;100

of
Hard

programme.<sup
id="cite_ref-123"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-123"><span>[</span>123<span>]</span></a></sup>
In
2011,
they
received
the
Innovator
Award
at
the
2011
<i><a
href="/wiki/Classic_Rock_(magazine)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Classic
Rock
(magazine)">Classic
Rock</a></i>
Awards
in
London.<sup
id="cite_ref-CRAward_17-1"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-CRAward-17"><span>[</span>17<span>]</span></a></sup>
A
<i><a

onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Rolling
Stone">Rolling
Stone</a></i>
readers'
poll
in
2012
ranked
<i><a
href="/wiki/Made_in_Japan_(Deep_Purple_album)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Made
in

(Deep
Purple

in
Japan</a></i>
the

of

<i><a

<i><a

<p>Prior
to
October
2012,
Deep
Purple
had
not
been
nominated
for
induction
into
the
<a
href="/wiki/Rock_and_Roll_Hall_of_Fame?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Rock
and
Roll
Hall
of
Fame">Rock
and
Roll
Hall
of
Fame</a>
(as
they've
been
eligible
since
1993),
but
were
nominated
for
induction
in
2012
and
2013.<sup
id="cite_ref-BillboardRHOF_125-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-BillboardRHOF-125"><span>[</span>125<span>]</span></a></sup><sup
id="cite_ref-126"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-126"><span>[</span>126<span>]</span></a></sup>
Despite
ranking
2nd
in
the
public's
vote
on
the
Rock
Hall
fans’
ballot,
which
had
over
half
a
million
votes,
they
were
not
inducted
by
the
Rock
Hall
committee.<sup
id="cite_ref-127"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-127"><span>[</span>127<span>]</span></a></sup>
<a
href="/wiki/Kiss_(band)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Kiss
(band)">Kiss</a>
bassist
<a
href="/wiki/Gene_Simmons?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Gene
Simmons">Gene
Simmons</a>
and
Rush
vocalist
<a
href="/wiki/Geddy_Lee?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Geddy
Lee">Geddy
Lee</a>
commented
that
Deep
Purple
should
obviously
be
among
the
Rock
and
Roll
Hall
of
Fame
inductees.<sup
id="cite_ref-Martin_Kielty_128-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Martin_Kielty-128"><span>[</span>128<span>]</span></a></sup><sup
id="cite_ref-129"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-129"><span>[</span>129<span>]</span></a></sup>
There
have
been
criticisms
in
the
past
over
Deep
Purple
not
having
been
inducted.
<a
href="/wiki/Toto_(band)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Toto
(band)">Toto</a>
guitarist
<a
href="/wiki/Steve_Lukather?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Steve
Lukather">Steve
Lukather</a>
commented,
&quot;they
put
<a
href="/wiki/Patti_Smith?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Patti
Smith">Patti
Smith</a>
in
there
but
not
Deep
Purple?
What's
the
first
song
every
kid
learns
how
to
play?
[&quot;Smoke
On
The
Water&quot;]...And
they're
not
in
the
Rock
and
Roll
Hall
of
Fame?
...the
Rock
and
Roll
Hall
of
Fame
has
lost
its
cool
because
of
the
glaring
omissions.&quot;<sup
id="cite_ref-130"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-130"><span>[</span>130<span>]</span></a></sup>
Former
<a
href="/wiki/Guns_N%27_Roses?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Guns
N'
Roses">Guns
N'
Roses</a>
guitarist
<a
href="/wiki/Slash_(musician)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Slash
(musician)">Slash</a>
expressed
his
surprise
and
disagreement
for
the
non-induction
of
Deep
Purple;
&quot;The
list
of
people
who
haven’t
even
been
nominated
is
mind-boggling..(the)
big
one
for
me
is
Deep
Purple.
How
could
you
not
induct
Deep
Purple?&quot;.<sup
id="cite_ref-131"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-131"><span>[</span>131<span>]</span></a></sup><sup
id="cite_ref-132"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-132"><span>[</span>132<span>]</span></a></sup>
When
asked
what
band
he'd
like
to
see
inducted
into
the
Rock
Hall,
Metallica
drummer
<a
href="/wiki/Lars_Ulrich?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Lars
Ulrich">Lars
Ulrich</a>
also
singled
out
Deep
Purple.<sup
id="cite_ref-133"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-133"><span>[</span>133<span>]</span></a></sup>
Metallica
guitarist
<a
href="/wiki/Kirk_Hammett?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Kirk
Hammett">Kirk
Hammett</a>
commented:
&quot;I've
been
lobbying
for
Deep
Purple
for
a
long,
long
time.
If
Black
Sabbath
can
be
in
the
Rock
and
Roll
Hall
Of
Fame,
Deep
Purple
definitely
belongs
in
the
Rock
And
Roll
Hall
Of
Fame.
'Cause
they
had
great
songs,
great
musicianship,
they
had
an
impact,
and
they're
a
huge
influence
on
the
heavy
metal
community
as
a
whole.
So
I
definitely
think
that
they
belong
in
the
Rock
and
Roll
Hall
Of
Fame.&quot;<sup
id="cite_ref-Kirk_Hammett_134-0"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Kirk_Hammett-134"><span>[</span>134<span>]</span></a></sup>
In
response
to
these,
a
Hall
of
Fame
chief
executive
said,
&quot;The
definition
of
‘rock
and
roll’
means
different
things
to
different
people,
but
as
broad
as
the
classifications
may
be,
they
all
share
a
common
love
of
the
music.&quot;<sup
id="cite_ref-Martin_Kielty_128-1"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Martin_Kielty-128"><span>[</span>128<span>]</span></a></sup>
Deep
Purple
vocalist
Ian
Gillan
also
commented,
&quot;To
us,
with
the
greatest
respect,
it
doesn't
mean
a
lot
although
it's
rather
like
an
award
in
the
U.K.,
if
I
were
to
get
one.
I
probably
wouldn't
accept
it.
But
then
again,
after
a
week
of
thinking
about
it,
I
would
accept
it
because
it
would
be
on
behalf
of
the
family
and
friends
and
everyone
who
supports
the
band
and
who's
looked
after
us
after
all
these
years.
It's
kind
of
a
recognition
of
everyone.
But
whether
we
deserve
it,
I
don't
know.
I
always
get
embarrassed
talking
about
this
stuff.&quot;<sup
id="cite_ref-Kirk_Hammett_134-1"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-Kirk_Hammett-134"><span>[</span>134<span>]</span></a></sup>
On
October
16,
2013
Deep
Purple
were
again
announced
as
nominees
for
inclusion
to
the
Hall.<sup
id="cite_ref-RS_2013_18-1"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-RS_2013-18"><span>[</span>18<span>]</span></a></sup></p>

<h2><span
class="mw-headline"
id="Concert_tours">Concert
tours</span>
<span
class="mw-editsection">[<a
href="/wiki?title=Deep_Purple&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11"
title="Edit
section:
Concert
tours">edit</a>]</span></h2>








<p>Deep
Purple
are
considered
to
be
one
of
the
hardest
touring
bands
in
the
world.<sup
id="cite_ref-135"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-135"><span>[</span>135<span>]</span></a></sup><sup
id="cite_ref-136"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-136"><span>[</span>136<span>]</span></a></sup><sup
id="cite_ref-137"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-137"><span>[</span>137<span>]</span></a></sup>
From
1968
until
today
(with
the
exception
of
their
1976–1984
split)
they
continue
to
tour
around
the
world.
In
2007,
the
band
received
a
special
award
for
selling
more
than
150,000
tickets
in
France,
with
40
dates
in
the
country
in
2007
alone.<sup
id="cite_ref-138"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-138"><span>[</span>138<span>]</span></a></sup>
Also
in
2007,
Deep
Purple's
<a
href="/wiki/Rapture_of_the_Deep_Tour?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Rapture
of
the
Deep
Tour"
class="mw-redirect">Rapture
of
the
Deep
Tour</a>
was
voted
number
6
concert
tour
of
the
year
(in
all
music
genres)
by
<a
href="/wiki/Planet_Rock_(radio_station)?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Planet
Rock
(radio
station)">Planet
Rock</a>
listeners.<sup
id="cite_ref-139"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-139"><span>[</span>139<span>]</span></a></sup>
<a
href="/wiki/The_Rolling_Stones?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="The
Rolling
Stones">The
Rolling
Stones</a>'
<a
href="/wiki/A_Bigger_Bang_Tour?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="A
Bigger
Bang
Tour"
class="mw-redirect">A
Bigger
Bang
Tour</a>
was
voted
number
5
and
beat
Purple's
tour
by
only
1%.
Deep
Purple
released
a
new
live
compilation
DVD
box,
Around
the
World
Live,
in
May
2008.
In
February
2008,
the
band
made
their
first
ever
appearance
at
the
Kremlin
Palace
in
Moscow,
Russia
<sup
id="cite_ref-140"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-140"><span>[</span>140<span>]</span></a></sup>
at
the
personal
request
of
Dmitry
Medvedev
who
at
the
time
was
considered
a
shoo-in
for
the
seat
of
the
Presidency
of
Russia.
Prior
to
that,
Deep
Purple
has
toured
Russia
several
times
starting
as
early
as
1987,
but
hasn't
played
a
venue
of
this
caliber.
The
band
was
part
of
the
entertainment
for
the
<a
href="/wiki/FIS_Nordic_World_Ski_Championships_2009?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="FIS
Nordic
World
Ski
Championships
2009">FIS
Nordic
World
Ski
Championships
2009</a>
in
<a
href="/wiki/Liberec?qsrc=3044"
onmousedown="triggerActionLog('primaryContent','','center','click','primaryContent','','');"
title="Liberec">Liberec</a>,
Czech
Republic.<sup
id="cite_ref-141"
class="reference"><a
href="#cite_note-141"><span>[</span>141<span>]</span></a></sup></p>

class="thumb
tright">

<script
type="text/javascript">




render_ads(false,
window['ad_config_bot']);





function
afc_match()
{








var
count
=
-1;








if(window['ad_config_top'])
{












count
=
window['ad_config_top'];








}









var
countBottom
=
0;








if(window['ad_config_bot'])
{












countBottom
=
window['ad_config_bot'];








}









if(window['backfillParam'])
{




























window['backfillParam']['pl_bmodn']
=
5;
























window['backfillParam']['pl_tnum']
=
count;












window['backfillParam']['pl_bnum']
=
countBottom;








}


































var
_matchUrl
=
"/afc-match?q=Deep_Purple&page=1&ac=24&qid=881D97E884ADF10283648A7B98480B92&qsrc=121&dm=&qrt=2&lid="+
"&o=0&l=dir&oo=&cl=ca-aj-cat&ch=cx_ask_wiki,ad_dirN";





















_matchUrl+=
"&userip=76.78.3.114";




































_matchUrl+="&losid=a&locid=encw&lodid=us&loaid=a16";









var
location
=
window.location
+
"";








location
=
location.substring(7);








var
cutIdx
=
location.indexOf("/");








if
(location.indexOf(":")
>
-1)
{




















cutIdx
=
1
+
cutIdx
+
location.substring(cutIdx+1).indexOf("/");








}









var
urlPrefix
=
location.substring(0,
cutIdx);








_matchUrl
=
"http://"
+
urlPrefix
+
_matchUrl
+
"&afcec="
+
count
+
"&afcecb="
+
countBottom;








ajax_get(_matchUrl,
null,
null);




}





function
getXHR()
{








if
(window.XMLHttpRequest)
{












return
new
XMLHttpRequest();








}
else
if
(window.ActiveXObject)
{












try
{
















return
new
ActiveXObject("Msxml2.XMLHTTP");












}
catch
(e)
{
















try
{




















return
new
ActiveXObject("Microsoft.XMLHTTP");
















}
catch
(E)
{




















return
null;
















}












}








}








else
{












return
null;








}




}





function
ajax_get(url,
onsuccess,
onerror)
{








var
obj
=
getXHR();








if(obj)
{












obj.onreadystatechange
=
function()
{
















if(obj.readyState==4)
{




















if
(obj.status
==
200
&&
typeof(onsuccess)
==
"function")
{
























onsuccess(obj);




















}
else
if
(typeof(onerror)
==
"function")
{
























onerror(obj);




















}






















try
{
























delete
obj['onreadystatechange'];




















}
catch(e)
{}
















}












};












obj.open("GET",
url,
true,
"",
"");












obj.send(null);












return
obj;








}
else
{












if(onerror)
{
















onerror("Error
creating
XHR");












}
else
{
















a10.debug("Error
creating
XHR");












}












return
null;








}




}





afc_match();

</script>
